         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
             <meta charset="UTF-8">
             <title>Book Details</title>
         </head>
         <body>
             <div id="book-details-page">
                 <h1 id="book-title">{{ book.title }}</h1>
                 <div id="book-author">Author: {{ book.author }}</div>
                 <div id="book-status">Status: {{ book.status }}</div>
                 <div id="book-description">Description: {{ book.description }}</div>
                 {% if book.status == 'Available' %}
                     <button id="borrow-button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('borrow_confirmation', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">Borrow</button>
                 {% else %}
                     <button id="borrow-button" disabled>Borrow</button>
                 {% endif %}
         
                 <div id="reviews-section">
                     <h2>Reviews</h2>
                     {% for review in reviews %}
                     <div class="review" id="review-{{ review.review_id }}">
                         <b>{{ review.username }}</b> ({{ review.review_date }}) - Rating: {{ review.rating }}/5
                         <p>{{ review.review_text }}</p>
                     </div>
                     {% else %}
                     <div>No reviews yet.</div>
                     {% endfor %}
                 </div>
         
                 {% if user_has_borrowed %}
                     <button id="write-review-button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('write_review', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">Write Review</button>
                 {% else %}
                     <button id="write-review-button" disabled>Write Review</button>
                 {% endif %}
         
                 <button id="back-to-catalog" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('book_catalog') }}'">Back to Catalog</button>
             </div>
         </body>
         </html>

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
             <meta charset="UTF-8">
             <title>Borrow Confirmation</title>
         </head>
         <body>
             <div id="borrow-page">
                 <div id="borrow-book-info">
                     <h2>{{ book.title }}</h2>
                     <div>Author: {{ book.author }}</div>
                     <div>Status: {{ book.status }}</div>
                 </div>
                 <div id="due-date-display">Due Date: {{ due_date }}</div>
                 <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book.book_id) }}">
                     <button id="confirm-borrow-button" type="submit">Confirm Borrow</button>
                     <button id="cancel-borrow-button" type="button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('book_details', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">Cancel</button>
                 </form>
             </div>
         </body>
         </html>

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
             <meta charset="UTF-8">
             <title>My Borrowings</title>
         </head>
         <body>
             <div id="my-borrows-page">
                 <label for="filter-status">Filter by status:</label>
                 <select id="filter-status">
                     <option value="All">All</option>
                     <option value="Active">Active</option>
                     <option value="Returned">Returned</option>
                     <option value="Overdue">Overdue</option>
                 </select>
         
                 <table id="borrows-table" border="1">
                     <thead>
                         <tr>
                             <th>Book Title</th>
                             <th>Borrow Date</th>
                             <th>Due Date</th>
                             <th>Status</th>
                             <th>Action</th>
                         </tr>
                     </thead>
                     <tbody>
                         {% for borrow in borrowings %}
                         <tr>
                             <td>{{ borrow.book_title }}</td>
                             <td>{{ borrow.borrow_date }}</td>
                             <td>{{ borrow.due_date }}</td>
                             <td>{{ borrow.status }}</td>
                             <td>
                                 {% if borrow.status == 'Active' %}
                                 <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('return_book', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id) }}">
                                     <button id="return-book-button-{{ borrow.borrow_id }}" type="submit">Return</button>
                                 </form>
                                 {% else %}
                                 <button id="return-book-button-{{ borrow.borrow_id }}" disabled>Return</button>
                                 {% endif %}
                             </td>
                         </tr>
                         {% endfor %}
                     </tbody>
                 </table>
         
                 <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
             </div>
         </body>
         </html>

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
             <meta charset="UTF-8">
             <title>My Reservations</title>
         </head>
         <body>
             <div id="reservations-page">
                 <table id="reservations-table" border="1">
                     <thead>
                         <tr>
                             <th>Book Title</th>
                             <th>Reservation Date</th>
                             <th>Status</th>
                             <th>Action</th>
                         </tr>
                     </thead>
                     <tbody>
                         {% for reservation in reservations %}
                         <tr>
                             <td>{{ reservation.book_title }}</td>
                             <td>{{ reservation.reservation_date }}</td>
                             <td>{{ reservation.status }}</td>
                             <td>

  [1] Agent: BackendDeveloper
      File: /home/jun/0624/CaMP_0327_backup/results/Software-web-rebuttal/compound_maxfailover_3/OnlineLibrary/compound_chaos/app.py

      Before (full content):
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, flash
         from datetime import datetime, timedelta
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'some_secret_key_for_sessions'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions for data I/O
         
         def read_users():
             users = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return users
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 4:
                         continue
                     username, email, phone, address = parts
                     users[username] = {
                         'username': username,
                         'email': email,
                         'phone': phone,
                         'address': address
                     }
             return users
         
         def write_users(users):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for u in users.values():
                         f.write(f"{u['username']}|{u['email']}|{u['phone']}|{u['address']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_books():
             books = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return books
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 10:
                         continue
                     try:
                         book_id = int(parts[0])
                         title = parts[1]
                         author = parts[2]
                         isbn = parts[3]
                         genre = parts[4]
                         publisher = parts[5]
                         year = int(parts[6])
                         description = parts[7]
                         status = parts[8]
                         avg_rating = float(parts[9])
                         books[book_id] = {
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'author': author,
                             'isbn': isbn,
                             'genre': genre,
                             'publisher': publisher,
                             'year': year,
                             'description': description,
                             'status': status,
                             'avg_rating': avg_rating
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return books
         
         def write_books(books):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in books.values():
                         f.write(f"{b['book_id']}|{b['title']}|{b['author']}|{b['isbn']}|{b['genre']}|{b['publisher']}|{b['year']}|{b['description']}|{b['status']}|{b['avg_rating']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_borrowings():
             borrowings = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return borrowings
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 8:
                         continue
                     try:
                         borrow_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         borrow_date = parts[3]
                         due_date = parts[4]
                         return_date = parts[5] if parts[5] else ''
                         status = parts[6]
                         fine_amount = float(parts[7])
                         borrowings[borrow_id] = {
                             'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                             'due_date': due_date,
                             'return_date': return_date,
                             'status': status,
                             'fine_amount': fine_amount
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return borrowings
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in borrowings.values():
                         return_date = b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                         f.write(f"{b['borrow_id']}|{b['username']}|{b['book_id']}|{b['borrow_date']}|{b['due_date']}|{return_date}|{b['status']}|{b['fine_amount']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_reservations():
             reservations = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reservations
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 5:
                         continue
                     try:
                         reservation_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         reservation_date = parts[3]
                         status = parts[4]
                         reservations[reservation_id] = {
                             'reservation_id': reservation_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'reservation_date': reservation_date,
                             'status': status
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return reservations
         
         def write_reservations(reservations):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reservations.values():
                         f.write(f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['reservation_date']}|{r['status']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_reviews():
             reviews = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reviews
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         review_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         rating = int(parts[3])
                         review_text = parts[4]
                         review_date = parts[5]
                         reviews[review_id] = {
                             'review_id': review_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'review_text': review_text,
                             'review_date': review_date
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return reviews
         
         def write_reviews(reviews):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reviews.values():
                         f.write(f"{r['review_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_fines():
             fines = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return fines
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         fine_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         borrow_id = int(parts[2])
                         amount = float(parts[3])
                         status = parts[4]
                         date_issued = parts[5]
                         fines[fine_id] = {
                             'fine_id': fine_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                             'amount': amount,
                             'status': status,
                             'date_issued': date_issued
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return fines
         
         def write_fines(fines):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for fine in fines.values():
                         f.write(f"{fine['fine_id']}|{fine['username']}|{fine['borrow_id']}|{fine['amount']}|{fine['status']}|{fine['date_issued']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         # Dummy user login simulation
         # For the purpose of this backend, we simulate a logged-in user by a constant
         # In real scenario, this would be session-based or auth based
         
         def get_current_username():
             # For demonstration, the username is fixed
             return 'john_reader'
         
         
         # Routes implementation
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_current_username()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username)
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def book_catalog():
             books_map = read_books()
             # We need to pass books list with required fields: book_id, title, author, status
             books = []
             for b in books_map.values():
                 books.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': b['title'],
                     'author': b['author'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books)
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
             # filter reviews for this book
             reviews = []
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'username': r['username'],
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'review_date': r['review_date']
                     })
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             user_has_borrowed = False
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active':
                     user_has_borrowed = True
                     break
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'status': book['status']
             }
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book_info, reviews=reviews, user_has_borrowed=user_has_borrowed)
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>')
         def borrow_confirmation(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book is not available for borrowing.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
             due_date = (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'status': book['status']
             }
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book_info, due_date=due_date)
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_borrow(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 message = 'Book not found.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=None, due_date=None, message=message)
         
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 message = 'Book is not available for borrowing.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=None, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             # Check if user already has an active borrow of this book
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active':
                     message = 'You already have this book borrowed.'
                     due_date = b['due_date']
                     return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
             # Create new borrow entry
             new_borrow_id = max(borrowings_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
             borrow_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date_dt = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)
             due_date = due_date_dt.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             new_borrowing = {
                 'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,
                 'username': current_user,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                 'due_date': due_date,
                 'return_date': '',
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             }
         
             borrowings_map[new_borrow_id] = new_borrowing
         
             # Update book status to Borrowed
             book['status'] = 'Borrowed'
         
             # Save updated data
             if not write_borrowings(borrowings_map) or not write_books(books_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update records.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
             message = f'Borrowing successful! Due date is {due_date}.'
             return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=True, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-borrows')
         def my_borrows():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             # filter borrowings for current user
             user_borrowings = []
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user:
                     book_title = books_map.get(b['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     # Determine status to ensure overdue handled?
                     # Confirm status consistent
                     # Statuses: Active, Returned, Overdue
                     user_borrowings.append({
                         'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'due_date': b['due_date'],
                         'status': b['status']
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrowings=user_borrowings)
         
         @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_book(borrow_id):
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             borrowing = borrowings_map.get(borrow_id)
             if not borrowing:
                 message = 'Borrowing record not found.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             if borrowing['username'] != current_user:
                 message = 'You are not authorized to return this book.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             if borrowing['status'] != 'Active' and borrowing['status'] != 'Overdue':
                 message = f'Cannot return book because borrowing status is {borrowing["status"]}.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             # Update borrow record: set return_date, status
             return_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             borrowing['return_date'] = return_date
             borrowing['status'] = 'Returned'
         
             # Update book status to Available
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(borrowing['book_id'])
             if book:
                 book['status'] = 'Available'
         
             # If overdue, calculate fine and create/update fine record
             fine_amount = 0.0
             due_date_dt = datetime.strptime(borrowing['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
             return_date_dt = datetime.strptime(return_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
             if return_date_dt > due_date_dt:
                 days_late = (return_date_dt - due_date_dt).days
                 fine_amount = days_late * 1.0  # Assuming $1 per day late
                 borrowing['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
         
                 fines_map = read_fines()
                 # check if a fine already exists for this borrow_id
                 fine_found = False
                 for fine in fines_map.values():
                     if fine['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                         fine['amount'] = fine_amount
                         fine['status'] = 'Unpaid'
                         fine['date_issued'] = return_date
                         fine_found = True
                         break
                 if not fine_found:
                     new_fine_id = max(fines_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
                     fines_map[new_fine_id] = {
                         'fine_id': new_fine_id,
                         'username': current_user,
                         'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                         'amount': fine_amount,
                         'status': 'Unpaid',
                         'date_issued': return_date
                     }
                 write_fines(fines_map)
             else:
                 borrowing['fine_amount'] = 0.0
         
             # Save updated borrowings and books
             if not write_borrowings(borrowings_map) or not write_books(books_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update return records.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             message = 'Book returned successfully.'
             return render_template('return_result.html', success=True, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-reservations')
         def my_reservations():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reservations_map = read_reservations()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             user_reservations = []
             for r in reservations_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user:
                     book_title = books_map.get(r['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     user_reservations.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                         'status': r['status']
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=user_reservations)
         
         @app.route('/cancel-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservations_map = read_reservations()
             reservation = reservations_map.get(reservation_id)
             if not reservation:
                 message = 'Reservation not found.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             if reservation['username'] != current_user:
                 message = 'You are not authorized to cancel this reservation.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             if reservation['status'] == 'Cancelled':
                 message = 'Reservation is already cancelled.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             reservation['status'] = 'Cancelled'
         
             if not write_reservations(reservations_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update reservation status.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             message = 'Reservation cancelled successfully.'
             return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=True, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-reviews')
         def my_reviews():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user:
                     book_title = books_map.get(r['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     user_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'book_id': r['book_id']
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)
         
         @app.route('/write-review/<int:book_id>')
         def write_review(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
         
             existing_review = None
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     existing_review = {
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text']
                     }
                     break
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description']
             }
         
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book_info, existing_review=existing_review)
         
         @app.route('/write-review/<int:book_id>/submit', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_review(book_id):
             current_user = get_current_username()
             rating_str = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text','').strip()
         
             message = ''
             success = False
         
             try:
                 rating = int(rating_str)
                 if rating < 1 or rating > 5:
                     raise ValueError
             except:
                 message = 'Rating must be an integer between 1 and 5.'
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             if not review_text:
                 message = 'Review text cannot be empty.'
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
         
             # check if review exists for this user and book
             existing_review_id = None
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     existing_review_id = r['review_id']
                     break
         
             review_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             if existing_review_id is not None:
                 # update existing review
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['rating'] = rating
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['review_text'] = review_text
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['review_date'] = review_date
                 message = 'Review updated successfully.'
                 success = True
             else:
                 # create new review
                 new_review_id = max(reviews_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
                 reviews_map[new_review_id] = {
                     'review_id': new_review_id,
                     'username': current_user,
                     'book_id': book_id,
                     'rating': rating,
                     'review_text': review_text,
                     'review_date': review_date
                 }
                 message = 'Review submitted successfully.'
                 success = True
         
             if not write_reviews(reviews_map):
                 message = 'Failed to write review.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=success, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             users_map = read_users()
             user = users_map.get(current_user)
             if not user:
                 flash('User not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             borrow_history = []
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user:
                     # Only include returned borrow or all borrowings?
                     # Spec: All previously borrowed books. We assume including returned.
                     book_title = books_map.get(b['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     borrow_history.append({
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                     })
         
             return render_template('profile.html',
                                    username=current_user,
                                    email=user.get('email',''),
                                    borrow_history=borrow_history)
         
         @app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             users_map = read_users()
             user = users_map.get(current_user)
             if not user:
                 message = 'User not found.'
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             # Update user info
             user['email'] = email if email else user['email']
             user['phone'] = phone if phone else user['phone']
             user['address'] = address if address else user['address']
         
             if write_users(users_map):
                 message = 'Profile updated successfully.'
                 success = True
             else:
                 message = 'Failed to update profile.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=success, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>')
         def payment_confirmation(fine_id):
             fines_map = read_fines()
             fine = fines_map.get(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
         
             fine_amount = fine['amount']
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine_amount=fine_amount, fine_id=fine_id)
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fines_map = read_fines()
             fine = fines_map.get(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 message = 'Fine record not found.'
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             if fine['status'] == 'Paid':
                 message = 'Fine already paid.'
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             fine['status'] = 'Paid'
             if write_fines(fines_map):
                 message = 'Payment successful. Thank you!'
                 success = True
             else:
                 message = 'Failed to update payment status.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('payment_result.html', success=success, message=message)

IO Chaos Content Corruptions (1 total):

  [1] Agent: BackendDeveloper
      Type: IO_CHAOS_WORD_SHUFFLE
      Details: WordShuffle: 1829 words shuffled across document

      Before (full content):
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, flash
         from datetime import datetime, timedelta
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'some_secret_key_for_sessions'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions for data I/O
         
         def read_users():
             users = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return users
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 4:
                         continue
                     username, email, phone, address = parts
                     users[username] = {
                         'username': username,
                         'email': email,
                         'phone': phone,
                         'address': address
                     }
             return users
         
         def write_users(users):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for u in users.values():
                         f.write(f"{u['username']}|{u['email']}|{u['phone']}|{u['address']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_books():
             books = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return books
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 10:
                         continue
                     try:
                         book_id = int(parts[0])
                         title = parts[1]
                         author = parts[2]
                         isbn = parts[3]
                         genre = parts[4]
                         publisher = parts[5]
                         year = int(parts[6])
                         description = parts[7]
                         status = parts[8]
                         avg_rating = float(parts[9])
                         books[book_id] = {
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'author': author,
                             'isbn': isbn,
                             'genre': genre,
                             'publisher': publisher,
                             'year': year,
                             'description': description,
                             'status': status,
                             'avg_rating': avg_rating
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return books
         
         def write_books(books):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in books.values():
                         f.write(f"{b['book_id']}|{b['title']}|{b['author']}|{b['isbn']}|{b['genre']}|{b['publisher']}|{b['year']}|{b['description']}|{b['status']}|{b['avg_rating']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_borrowings():
             borrowings = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return borrowings
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 8:
                         continue
                     try:
                         borrow_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         borrow_date = parts[3]
                         due_date = parts[4]
                         return_date = parts[5] if parts[5] else ''
                         status = parts[6]
                         fine_amount = float(parts[7])
                         borrowings[borrow_id] = {
                             'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                             'due_date': due_date,
                             'return_date': return_date,
                             'status': status,
                             'fine_amount': fine_amount
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return borrowings
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in borrowings.values():
                         return_date = b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                         f.write(f"{b['borrow_id']}|{b['username']}|{b['book_id']}|{b['borrow_date']}|{b['due_date']}|{return_date}|{b['status']}|{b['fine_amount']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_reservations():
             reservations = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reservations
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 5:
                         continue
                     try:
                         reservation_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         reservation_date = parts[3]
                         status = parts[4]
                         reservations[reservation_id] = {
                             'reservation_id': reservation_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'reservation_date': reservation_date,
                             'status': status
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return reservations
         
         def write_reservations(reservations):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reservations.values():
                         f.write(f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['reservation_date']}|{r['status']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_reviews():
             reviews = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reviews
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         review_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         book_id = int(parts[2])
                         rating = int(parts[3])
                         review_text = parts[4]
                         review_date = parts[5]
                         reviews[review_id] = {
                             'review_id': review_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'book_id': book_id,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'review_text': review_text,
                             'review_date': review_date
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return reviews
         
         def write_reviews(reviews):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reviews.values():
                         f.write(f"{r['review_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         def read_fines():
             fines = {}
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return fines
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line: continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         fine_id = int(parts[0])
                         username = parts[1]
                         borrow_id = int(parts[2])
                         amount = float(parts[3])
                         status = parts[4]
                         date_issued = parts[5]
                         fines[fine_id] = {
                             'fine_id': fine_id,
                             'username': username,
                             'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                             'amount': amount,
                             'status': status,
                             'date_issued': date_issued
                         }
                     except:
                         continue
             return fines
         
         def write_fines(fines):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for fine in fines.values():
                         f.write(f"{fine['fine_id']}|{fine['username']}|{fine['borrow_id']}|{fine['amount']}|{fine['status']}|{fine['date_issued']}\n")
                 return True
             except:
                 return False
         
         
         # Dummy user login simulation
         # For the purpose of this backend, we simulate a logged-in user by a constant
         # In real scenario, this would be session-based or auth based
         
         def get_current_username():
             # For demonstration, the username is fixed
             return 'john_reader'
         
         
         # Routes implementation
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_current_username()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username)
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def book_catalog():
             books_map = read_books()
             # We need to pass books list with required fields: book_id, title, author, status
             books = []
             for b in books_map.values():
                 books.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': b['title'],
                     'author': b['author'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books)
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
             # filter reviews for this book
             reviews = []
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'username': r['username'],
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'review_date': r['review_date']
                     })
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             user_has_borrowed = False
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active':
                     user_has_borrowed = True
                     break
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'status': book['status']
             }
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book_info, reviews=reviews, user_has_borrowed=user_has_borrowed)
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>')
         def borrow_confirmation(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book is not available for borrowing.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
             due_date = (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'status': book['status']
             }
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book_info, due_date=due_date)
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_borrow(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 message = 'Book not found.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=None, due_date=None, message=message)
         
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 message = 'Book is not available for borrowing.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=None, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             # Check if user already has an active borrow of this book
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active':
                     message = 'You already have this book borrowed.'
                     due_date = b['due_date']
                     return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
             # Create new borrow entry
             new_borrow_id = max(borrowings_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
             borrow_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date_dt = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)
             due_date = due_date_dt.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             new_borrowing = {
                 'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,
                 'username': current_user,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                 'due_date': due_date,
                 'return_date': '',
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             }
         
             borrowings_map[new_borrow_id] = new_borrowing
         
             # Update book status to Borrowed
             book['status'] = 'Borrowed'
         
             # Save updated data
             if not write_borrowings(borrowings_map) or not write_books(books_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update records.'
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
             message = f'Borrowing successful! Due date is {due_date}.'
             return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=True, book=book, due_date=due_date, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-borrows')
         def my_borrows():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             # filter borrowings for current user
             user_borrowings = []
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user:
                     book_title = books_map.get(b['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     # Determine status to ensure overdue handled?
                     # Confirm status consistent
                     # Statuses: Active, Returned, Overdue
                     user_borrowings.append({
                         'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'due_date': b['due_date'],
                         'status': b['status']
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrowings=user_borrowings)
         
         @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_book(borrow_id):
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             borrowing = borrowings_map.get(borrow_id)
             if not borrowing:
                 message = 'Borrowing record not found.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             if borrowing['username'] != current_user:
                 message = 'You are not authorized to return this book.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             if borrowing['status'] != 'Active' and borrowing['status'] != 'Overdue':
                 message = f'Cannot return book because borrowing status is {borrowing["status"]}.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             # Update borrow record: set return_date, status
             return_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             borrowing['return_date'] = return_date
             borrowing['status'] = 'Returned'
         
             # Update book status to Available
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(borrowing['book_id'])
             if book:
                 book['status'] = 'Available'
         
             # If overdue, calculate fine and create/update fine record
             fine_amount = 0.0
             due_date_dt = datetime.strptime(borrowing['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
             return_date_dt = datetime.strptime(return_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
             if return_date_dt > due_date_dt:
                 days_late = (return_date_dt - due_date_dt).days
                 fine_amount = days_late * 1.0  # Assuming $1 per day late
                 borrowing['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
         
                 fines_map = read_fines()
                 # check if a fine already exists for this borrow_id
                 fine_found = False
                 for fine in fines_map.values():
                     if fine['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                         fine['amount'] = fine_amount
                         fine['status'] = 'Unpaid'
                         fine['date_issued'] = return_date
                         fine_found = True
                         break
                 if not fine_found:
                     new_fine_id = max(fines_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
                     fines_map[new_fine_id] = {
                         'fine_id': new_fine_id,
                         'username': current_user,
                         'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                         'amount': fine_amount,
                         'status': 'Unpaid',
                         'date_issued': return_date
                     }
                 write_fines(fines_map)
             else:
                 borrowing['fine_amount'] = 0.0
         
             # Save updated borrowings and books
             if not write_borrowings(borrowings_map) or not write_books(books_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update return records.'
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
             message = 'Book returned successfully.'
             return render_template('return_result.html', success=True, borrow_id=borrow_id, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-reservations')
         def my_reservations():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reservations_map = read_reservations()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             user_reservations = []
             for r in reservations_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user:
                     book_title = books_map.get(r['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     user_reservations.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                         'status': r['status']
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=user_reservations)
         
         @app.route('/cancel-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservations_map = read_reservations()
             reservation = reservations_map.get(reservation_id)
             if not reservation:
                 message = 'Reservation not found.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             if reservation['username'] != current_user:
                 message = 'You are not authorized to cancel this reservation.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             if reservation['status'] == 'Cancelled':
                 message = 'Reservation is already cancelled.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             reservation['status'] = 'Cancelled'
         
             if not write_reservations(reservations_map):
                 message = 'Failed to update reservation status.'
                 return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=False, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
             message = 'Reservation cancelled successfully.'
             return render_template('cancellation_result.html', success=True, reservation_id=reservation_id, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/my-reviews')
         def my_reviews():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user:

                     })
         
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)
         
         @app.route('/write-review/<int:book_id>')
         def write_review(book_id):
             books_map = read_books()
             book = books_map.get(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             current_user = get_current_username()
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
         
             existing_review = None
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     existing_review = {
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text']
                     }
                     break
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description']
             }
         
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book_info, existing_review=existing_review)
         
         @app.route('/write-review/<int:book_id>/submit', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_review(book_id):
             current_user = get_current_username()
             rating_str = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text','').strip()
         
             message = ''
             success = False
         
             try:
                 rating = int(rating_str)
                 if rating < 1 or rating > 5:
                     raise ValueError
             except:
                 message = 'Rating must be an integer between 1 and 5.'
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             if not review_text:
                 message = 'Review text cannot be empty.'
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             reviews_map = read_reviews()
         
             # check if review exists for this user and book
             existing_review_id = None
             for r in reviews_map.values():
                 if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     existing_review_id = r['review_id']
                     break
         
             review_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             if existing_review_id is not None:
                 # update existing review
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['rating'] = rating
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['review_text'] = review_text
                 reviews_map[existing_review_id]['review_date'] = review_date
                 message = 'Review updated successfully.'
                 success = True
             else:
                 # create new review
                 new_review_id = max(reviews_map.keys(), default=0) + 1
                 reviews_map[new_review_id] = {
                     'review_id': new_review_id,
                     'username': current_user,
                     'book_id': book_id,
                     'rating': rating,
                     'review_text': review_text,
                     'review_date': review_date
                 }
                 message = 'Review submitted successfully.'
                 success = True
         
             if not write_reviews(reviews_map):
                 message = 'Failed to write review.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=success, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             users_map = read_users()
             user = users_map.get(current_user)
             if not user:
                 flash('User not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
             borrowings_map = read_borrowings()
             books_map = read_books()
         
             borrow_history = []
             for b in borrowings_map.values():
                 if b['username'] == current_user:
                     # Only include returned borrow or all borrowings?
                     # Spec: All previously borrowed books. We assume including returned.
                     book_title = books_map.get(b['book_id'], {}).get('title', 'Unknown')
                     borrow_history.append({
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                     })
         
             return render_template('profile.html',
                                    username=current_user,
                                    email=user.get('email',''),
                                    borrow_history=borrow_history)
         
         @app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             current_user = get_current_username()
             users_map = read_users()
             user = users_map.get(current_user)
             if not user:
                 message = 'User not found.'
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             # Update user info
             user['email'] = email if email else user['email']
             user['phone'] = phone if phone else user['phone']
             user['address'] = address if address else user['address']
         
             if write_users(users_map):
                 message = 'Profile updated successfully.'
                 success = True
             else:
                 message = 'Failed to update profile.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=success, message=message)
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>')
         def payment_confirmation(fine_id):
             fines_map = read_fines()
             fine = fines_map.get(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
         
             fine_amount = fine['amount']
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine_amount=fine_amount, fine_id=fine_id)
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fines_map = read_fines()
             fine = fines_map.get(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 message = 'Fine record not found.'
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             if fine['status'] == 'Paid':
                 message = 'Fine already paid.'
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message=message)
         
             fine['status'] = 'Paid'
             if write_fines(fines_map):
                 message = 'Payment successful. Thank you!'
                 success = True
             else:
                 message = 'Failed to update payment status.'
                 success = False
         
             return render_template('payment_result.html', success=success, message=message)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True,host='0.0.0.0', port=5000)
